<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ис-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">is-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:черпать.html>че́рпать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čérpatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***исчерпываться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:исчерпываться.html>исче́рпываться</a> (18987)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">исче́рпывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">isčérpyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исчерпываться.html>исче́рпываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">isčérpyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">исче́рпаться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be confined/reduced <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́тим</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:исчерпываться.html>исче́рпывается</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">étim délo ne <b>isčérpyvajetsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">this is not all there is to it; there is more to it than that</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">исче́рпывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">isčérpyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:итак.html>ита́к</a> (1492)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:итак.html>ита́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">iták</span>)
</p>

***итого.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:итого.html>итого́</a> (15604)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Univerbation of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">i</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>того́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tovó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:итого.html>итого́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">itovó</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>total, in total, in all</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:итог.html>ито́г</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">itóg</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<ol><li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;">бухг.</span>, <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="канцелярское">канц.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всего́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:итог.html>ито́ге</a> (<span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;">употр. <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:конец.html>конце́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:перечисление.html>перечисле́ния</a> каких-н. <a href = vnd.unilang:сумма.html>су́мм</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:количество.html>коли́честв</a></span>) <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>За</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ним</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:числиться.html>чи́слится</a> 100, 50 <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> 70 <a href = vnd.unilang:рубль.html>рубле́й</a> — <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:итого.html>итого́</a></span> 220 <a href = vnd.unilang:рубль.html>рубле́й</a>. </span></li>
</ul></li>


</ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:итог.html>ито́г</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">itóg</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:итоговый.html>ито́говый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">itógovyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>total, resultant
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:итоговый.html>ито́говая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сумма.html>су́мма</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>itógovaja</b> súmma</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sum total</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>total</b> sum</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>final, closing, concluding

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:итоговый.html>ито́говое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:занятие.html>заня́тие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>itógovoje</b> zanjátije</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>concluding</b> session</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ишак.html>иша́к</a> (17929)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> borrowing. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">eşek</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***ишь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ишь.html>ишь</a> (4915)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Contraction of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вишь.html>вишь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">višʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>., in turn <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">contraction of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:видеть.html>ви́дишь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vídišʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ишь.html>ишь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">išʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> see!; (just) look, listen; there; oh; now
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ишь.html>ишь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>išʹ</b> ty!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">how d'you like that!; oh come on!; what are you talking about!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><a href = vnd.unilang:частица.html>Части́ца</a><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>

***июль.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:июль.html>июль</a> (2498)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Greek">Byzantine Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Ιούλιος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Ioúlios</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">iūlius</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:июль.html>ию́ль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ijúlʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:июль.html>ию́ля</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:июль.html>ию́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:июль.html>ию́лей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>July
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:июль.html>ию́ле</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>ijúle</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">in July</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:июль.html>ию́ле</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>го́да</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>ijúle</b> étovo góda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in July</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:июль.html>ию́ле</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:прошлый.html>про́шлого</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>го́да</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>ijúle</b> próšlovo góda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">July of last year</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:июль.html>ию́ле</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:будущее.html>бу́дущего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>го́да</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>ijúle</b> búduščevo góda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">July of next year</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:июль.html>ию́ля</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">do <b>ijúlja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">until July</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:июль.html>ию́ля</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:декабрь.html>дека́брь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>ijúlja</b> po dekábrʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">from July to December</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:июль.html>ию́лю</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">k <b>ijúlju</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">by July</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвое</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:июль.html>ию́ля</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pérvoje <b>ijúlja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">July first</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвого</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:июль.html>ию́ля</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pérvovo <b>ijúlja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">on July first</span></div>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">1-го <b><a href = vnd.unilang:июль.html>ию́ля</a></b> 2010 г.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">1-go <b>ijúlja</b> 2010 g.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">July 1, 2010</span></div></li></ul></dd>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:июль.html>ию́ль</a></b> — <a href = vnd.unilang:макушка.html>маку́шка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>ле́та</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">saying</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ijúlʹ</b> — makúška léta</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">July is the head of summer</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:июль.html>ию́ле</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:двор.html>дворе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пустой.html>пу́сто</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пол.html>по́ле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:густой.html>гу́сто</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">saying</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>ijúle</b> na dvoré pústo, da na póle gústo</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">in July there is nothing on the farm, but all on the field</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:июль.html>ию́ль</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:хоть.html>хоть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:раздеться.html>разде́нься</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:декабрь.html>дека́брь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:потеплеть.html>потепле́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одеться.html>оде́нься</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">saying</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ijúlʹ</b> xotʹ razdénʹsja, a dekábrʹ potepléj odénʹsja</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">in July you may undress, but in December you must dress warmly (i.e. July is hottest month of the year, and December is coldest)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***июльский.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:июльский.html>ию́льский</a> (16417)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:июль.html>ию́ль</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ijúlʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:июльский.html>ию́льский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ijúlʹskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> July
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:июльский.html>ию́льский</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ijúlʹskij</b> denʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a July day</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:июльский.html>ию́льская</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:монархия.html>мона́рхия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Ijúlʹskaja</b> monárxija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the July Monarchy</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<table style="float:right; clear:right; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" width="210" class="morfotable ru">
<tbody><tr>

***июнь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:июнь.html>июнь</a> (2331)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">июнии</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ijunii</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Greek">Byzantine Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Ἰούνιος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Ioúnios</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">iūnius</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">Iūnō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Juno</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from (perhaps) <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*yuwn̥kós</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*yew-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">vital force, youthful vigor</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:июнь.html>ию́нь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ijúnʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:июнь.html>ию́ня</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:июнь.html>ию́ни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:июнь.html>ию́ней</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>June
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:июнь.html>ию́не</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>ijúne</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">in June</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:июнь.html>ию́не</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>го́да</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>ijúne</b> étovo góda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in June</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:июнь.html>ию́не</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:прошлый.html>про́шлого</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>го́да</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>ijúne</b> próšlovo góda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">June of last year</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:июнь.html>ию́не</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:будущее.html>бу́дущего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>го́да</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>ijúne</b> búduščevo góda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">June of next year</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:июнь.html>ию́ня</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">do <b>ijúnja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">until June</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:июнь.html>ию́ня</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:декабрь.html>дека́брь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>ijúnja</b> po dekábrʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">from June to December</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:июнь.html>ию́ню</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">k <b>ijúnju</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">by June</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвое</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:июнь.html>ию́ня</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pérvoje <b>ijúnja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">June first</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвого</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:июнь.html>ию́ня</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pérvovo <b>ijúnja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">on June first</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">1-го <b><a href = vnd.unilang:июнь.html>ию́ня</a></b> 2010 г.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">1-go <b>ijúnja</b> 2010 g.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">June 1, 2010</span></div></dd>

***к.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> (19)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Letter_4">Letter</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">k</span>) (<i>lower case</i>, <i>upper case</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>К</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The twelfth letter of the Russian Cyrillic alphabet. Its name is <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and it has the sound of English <b>k</b>. It is preceded by <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">Й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">J</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and followed by <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">Л</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">L</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kъ(n)</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">k</span>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ dative case</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to, toward
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>до́му</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>k</b> dómu</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to</b> the house</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:брат.html>бра́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>k</b> brátu</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to</b> (my) brother</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ко.html>ко</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ko</b> mne</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to</b> me</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>by, for <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of time</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ко.html>ко</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вторник.html>вто́рнику</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ko</b> vtórniku</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>by</b> Tuesday, <b>for</b> Tuesday</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ко.html>ко</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is used before words beginning with certain awkward consonant clusters such as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мн-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mn-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вс-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vs-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вт-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vt-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сн-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sn-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Abbreviation of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">кило-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kilo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кабак.html>кабак</a> (8540)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Kabacke</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hut, hovel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кабак.html>каба́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kabák</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кабак.html>кабака́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кабак.html>кабаки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кабак.html>кабако́в</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">каба́цкий</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>кабачо́к</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tavern, pub, <a href = vnd.unilang:бар.html>bar</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> watering hole, dive, joint
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грязный.html>гря́зный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кабак.html>каба́к</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">grjáznyj <b>kabák</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">crummy joint</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> borrowing, compare to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">kabak</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tatar language">Tatar</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="tt"><a href = vnd.unilang:кабак.html>кабак</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="tt-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">qabaq</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кабала.html>кабала́</a> (28443)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:кабала.html>кабала́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kabala</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">document, deed, debt issue</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">kabal</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">certain quantity, tasked labour, one day labour</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кабала.html>кабала́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kabalá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кабала.html>кабалы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кабала.html>кабалы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кабала.html>каба́л</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> promissory note, leading to debt bondage if unpaid</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> debt bondage</li>
<li>enslavement, servitude, bondage</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hebrew language">Hebrew</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">קַבָּלָה‎</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">receiving/tradition</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кабала.html>кабала́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kabalá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кабала.html>кабалы́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">religion</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> kabbalah</li></ol>

***кабан.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кабан.html>кабан</a> (7843)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> language (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tatar language">Tatar</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tt">kaban</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Azerbaijani_language" class="extiw" title="w:Azerbaijani language">Azerbaijani</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="az">qaban</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kazakh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Kazakh language">Kazakh</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="kk">қабан</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="kk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">qaban</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>); cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">yaban</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кабан.html>каба́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kabán</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кабан.html>кабана́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кабан.html>кабаны́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кабан.html>кабано́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>boar, wild boar</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вепрь.html>вепрь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">veprʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сека́ч</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sekáč</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>кабачок</a> (13771)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кабак.html>каба́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kabák</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tavern, pub, <a href = vnd.unilang:бар.html>bar</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ок</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>кабачо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kabačók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кабачок.html>кабачка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кабачок.html>кабачки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кабачок.html>кабачко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кабак.html>каба́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kabák</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tavern, pub, <a href = vnd.unilang:бар.html>bar</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li>little pub, little restaurant, saloon</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> <i class="Zyyy mention" lang="und">kapgak</i>, <i class="Zyyy mention" lang="und">kapak</i>  + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ок</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">kabak</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">marrow, squash</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>кабачо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kabačók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кабачок.html>кабачка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кабачок.html>кабачки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кабачок.html>кабачко́в</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">кабачко́вый</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>vegetable marrow, squash, zucchini</li></ol>
